<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступать.html>ступа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вступать.html>вступа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstupátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вступить.html>вступи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to enter, to march into (of the troops)</li>
<li>to join (to become a member of)</li>
<li>to begin, to start, to assume
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вступать.html>вступа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vstupátʹ</b> v déjstvije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to come into operation</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***вступивший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вступить.html>вступи́вший</a> (2413)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вступить.html>вступи́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstupívšij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вступить.html>вступи́ть</a> (2413)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступить.html>ступи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вступить.html>вступи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vstupítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вступать.html>вступа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to enter, to march into (of the troops)</li>
<li>to join, to enlist</li>
<li>to begin, to start, to assume
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вступить.html>вступи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vstupítʹ</b> v déjstvije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to come into operation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вступить.html>вступи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брак.html>брак</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vstupítʹ</b> v brak</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to marry</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">

***всхлипывание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:всхлипывание.html>всхли́пывание</a> (24892)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всхлипывать.html>всхли́пывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vsxlípyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ание</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всхлипывание.html>всхли́пывание</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vsxlípyvanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всхлипывание.html>всхли́пывания</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всхлипывание.html>всхли́пывания</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всхлипывание.html>всхли́пываний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sobbing, weeping, sobs</li></ol>

***всходить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:всходить.html>всходи́ть</a> (16685)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всходить.html>всходи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vsxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взойти.html>взойти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to mount, to go up, to climb, to ascend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a heavenly body</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rise
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заходить.html>заходи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaxodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sadítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of plants</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come up, to sprout</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:всякое.html>вся́кий</a> (1155)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">вьсакъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vĭsakŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">уся́кий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usjákyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">уся́кі</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">usjáki</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">все́ки</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vséki</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">сва̏к</i> / <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">svȁk</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всякое.html>вся́кий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vsjákij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>any, every</li>
<li>all sorts of</li>
<li>all kinds of</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всякое.html>вся́кий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vsjákij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>anybody, anyone, everybody, everyone</li>
<li>anything</li></ol>

***втаскивавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:втаскивавший.html>вта́скивавший</a> (31101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:втаскивавший.html>вта́скивавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vtáskivavšij</span>)
